          <div class="t withAv">
           It would be nice if that was all there was to it, but there's too much (potential) symbolism involved.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           For my part I would try to judge the situation.  If a woman asked me to hold her purse for just a moment and it seemed like a reasonable request without any hidden meaning behind it, I'd do it.  But if I sense that she could just as easily set it down somewhere, or she wants me to carry it around for awhile, or her girlfriends are watching, I'm going to suspect that she's "testing" me to see if I'll just meekly obey her even if she asks me to do something emasculating.  Girls don't like guys who are pushovers and they respect men more who stand up to them, so in that circumstance I'd just say no.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Some people might say that's over-thinking it, but I think men have to be aware of their image because women ruthlessly judge them on it.  Just having good intentions won't get you anywhere as a man.
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
